function SetCookie(c_name,value,expiredays)
{
var exdate=new Date()
exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate()+expiredays)
document.cookie=c_name+ "=" +escape(value)+";path=/"+((expiredays==null) ? "" : ";expires="+exdate.toUTCString())
}
 
        $(document).ready(function() {
            <!-- -->$(".dropdown img.flag").addClass("flagvisibility");

            $(".dropdown dt a").click(function() {
                $(".dropdown dd ul").toggle();
            });
                        
            $(".dropdown dd ul li a").click(function() {
                var text = $(this).html();
                $(".dropdown dt a span").html(text);
                $(".dropdown dd ul").hide();
                $("#result").html("Selected value is: " + getSelectedValue("sample"));
            });
                        
            function getSelectedValue(id) {
                return $("#" + id).find("dt a span.value").html();
            }

            $(document).bind('click', function(e) {
                var $clicked = $(e.target);
                if (! $clicked.parents().hasClass("dropdown"))
                    $(".dropdown dd ul").hide();
            });


            $("#flagSwitcher").click(function() {
                $(".dropdown img.flag").toggleClass("flagvisibility");
            });
        });


function verifysrch(){
 
	var srchv=document.getElementById("query").value;if((srchv.length==0)||(srchv.length==1)||(srchv=="product code or keyword")){
		alert("Veuillez entrer un minimum de 2 caractères");
		return false;
		}
 
}        
      
function verifysrch2(input_name){
 
	var srchv=document.getElementById(input_name).value;
	if((srchv.length==0)||(srchv.length==1)){
		alert("Veuillez entrer un minimum de 2 caractères");
		return false;
		}
 
}
function txtvalid(frm) {
    if (frm.desc.value.length == 0)
    {
        alert("Please enter a search word.")
        frm.desc.focus()
        return false
    }
}
function prdvalid(frm) {
    if (frm.prod_pref.value.length < 3)
    {
        alert("Please enter a product code. It must contain at least six characters.")
        frm.prod_pref.focus()
        return false
    }
}
function noitems() {
	alert("Your basket is currently empty.");
	}

function popupimg(img, pref, suff, pic) {
	var path = "/zoom.jsp?img=" + img + "\&pref=" + pref + "\&suff=" + suff + "\&pic=" + pic;
	imgzoom = window.open(path, "imgzoom", "scrollbars=no, status=no, scrolling=no, width=640, height=600");
	imgzoom.focus();
}

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
function chkvals(formnum){   

var qty = parseInt(formnum.Quantity.value);
if(formnum.conspec.value){
var jsconspec= parseInt(formnum.conspec.value);}
err_msg = "";
valsok=1;


  if ( isNaN (qty) || formnum.Quantity.value.indexOf(".") != -1) {
   err_msg = err_msg + "Veuillez entrer un nombre valide pour la quantité.\n";

   linkClicked=0;
valsok=0;

}
 if(formnum.conspec.value){
if (qty % parseInt(jsconspec) != 0){
err_msg = err_msg + "Le prix indiqué est le prix unitaire. Ce produit est vendu par boite de"+" "+ jsconspec +".\n"+"Merci de saisir comme quantité"+" "+jsconspec+", "+"ou un multiple de"+" "+jsconspec +" si vous désirez plusieurs boites.\n";

   linkClicked=0;
valsok=0;
}
}
if(formnum.discontinuestat.value.indexOf("S") != -1){

err_msg = err_msg + "Ce produit n'est pas disponible sur le site internet. Veuillez contacter votre agence pour connaitre le stock local. \n";

   linkClicked=0;
valsok=0;

}
if(formnum.discontinuestat.value.indexOf("A") != -1){

err_msg = err_msg + "Ce produit n'est pas disponible sur le site internet. Veuillez contacter votre agence pour connaitre le stock local. \n";

   linkClicked=0;
valsok=0;

}
 
if (qty > 999999 || qty < 1){
   err_msg = err_msg + "Veuillez indiquer une quantité comprise entre 0 et 999999\n";

   linkClicked=0;



valsok=0;
  }

 

if (valsok == 1) {
	facebook_pixel(formnum.prod_prefix.value.trim() + " " + formnum.prod_suffix.value.trim(), formnum.myprice.value );
  return true;
} else {
//   err_msg = err_msg + "Invalide.";
   alert(err_msg);
   linkClicked=0;
  return false;
}

}


function facebook_pixel(my_id, my_price){
	
	fbq('track', 'AddToCart', {
		content_ids: [my_id],
		content_type: 'product',
		value: my_price,
		currency: 'EUR'
	});
}

function openPopup(e){
	
	popup = $(e).attr("rel");
	popup360 = $(e).attr("rel2");
	
	$('#' + popup).css("display","block");
	
	if (popup == "pop_video_player") {
	if(Browser.isIE){
	  $('#cust-video-99').remove();}
	var vdeo = " ";
	vdeo += "<object width=\"700\" height=\"425\">";
	vdeo+= "<param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/" + popup360 + "&autoplay=1&rel=0\"></param>";
	vdeo+= "<param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\"></param><param name=\"allowscriptaccess\" value=\"always\"></param>";
	vdeo+= "<embed src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/" + popup360 + "&autoplay=1&rel=0\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowscriptaccess=\"always\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" width=\"700\" height=\"425\"></embed>";
	vdeo+= "</object>";
	vdeo+= "</div>";
    var vdsp = $("<div id=\"cust-video-99\">").html(vdeo);
  
	$(vdsp).insertAfter('#video1');
	video1.remove();
	
	} else	if (popup == "pop_interactive_player") {
	
	var img_nam = "/flash/prods/" + popup360 + ".swf";
	
		var so = new SWFObject(img_nam, popup360, "400", "300", "8");
		so.write("flash1");

	} else {
        var h360 = "<object classid=\"clsid:d27cdb6e-ae6d-11cf-96b8-444553540000\" width=\"420\" height=\"420\" id=\"Player\" align=\"middle\">";
		h360+= "<param name=\"movie\" value=\"https://rotaryview.com/flashPlayer/player/Player.swf\"/>";
		h360+= "<param name=\"flashvars\" value=\"movID=" + popup360 + "&width=420&height=420&ext=true\"/>";
		h360+= "<param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\"/>";
		h360+= "<!--[if !IE]>--><object type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" data=\"https://rotaryview.com/flashPlayer/player/Player.swf\" width=\"420\" height=\"420\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"https://rotaryview.com/flashPlayer/player/Player.swf\"/><param name=\"flashvars\" value=\"movID=" + popup360 + "&width=420&height=420&ext=true\"/><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\"/><img src=\"http://d2nh5z7fuzzi9h.cloudfront.net/media/lores/59213539/0000_2.jpg\" alt=\"\"/></object><!--<![endif]-->";
		h360+= "</object>";
		h360+= "<p>360</p></div>";
//		h360.write("flash2");
        var p360 = $("<div id=\"360\">").html(h360);
        $(p360).insertAfter('#flash2');
	flash2.remove();
	
	}
	
	
}

function closePopups(){
	
	$('.b_popup').css("display","none");
	$('.b_image_popup').css("display","none");
	$('.b_video_popup').css("display","none");
	$('.pop_deliveryhaz').css("display","none");
	$('.b_interactive_popup').css("display","none");
	$('.b_interactive_popup2').css("display","none");
	$('.atb-modal').css("display","none");
	$('.atb-bg').css("display","none");
		
		
}

<script type="text/javascript">
		$(document).ready(function() {
			/*
			 *  Simple image gallery. Uses default settings
			 */

			$('.fancybox').fancybox();

			/*
			 *  Different effects
			 */

			// Change title type, overlay closing speed
			$(".fancybox-effects-a").fancybox({
				helpers: {
					title : {
						type : 'outside'
					},
					overlay : {
						speedOut : 0
					}
				}
			});

			// Disable opening and closing animations, change title type
			$(".fancybox-effects-b").fancybox({
				openEffect  : 'none',
				closeEffect	: 'none',

				helpers : {
					title : {
						type : 'over'
					}
				}
			});

			// Set custom style, close if clicked, change title type and overlay color
			$(".fancybox-effects-c").fancybox({
				wrapCSS    : 'fancybox-custom',
				closeClick : true,

				openEffect : 'none',

				helpers : {
					title : {
						type : 'inside'
					},
					overlay : {
						css : {
							'background' : 'rgba(238,238,238,0.85)'
						}
					}
				}
			});

			// Remove padding, set opening and closing animations, close if clicked and disable overlay
			$(".fancybox-effects-d").fancybox({
				padding: 0,

				openEffect : 'elastic',
				openSpeed  : 150,

				closeEffect : 'elastic',
				closeSpeed  : 150,

				closeClick : true,

				helpers : {
					overlay : null
				}
			});

			/*
			 *  Button helper. Disable animations, hide close button, change title type and content
			 */

			$('.fancybox-buttons').fancybox({
				openEffect  : 'none',
				closeEffect : 'none',

				prevEffect : 'none',
				nextEffect : 'none',

				closeBtn  : false,

				helpers : {
					title : {
						type : 'inside'
					},
					buttons	: {}
				},

				afterLoad : function() {
					this.title = 'Image ' + (this.index + 1) + ' of ' + this.group.length + (this.title ? ' - ' + this.title : '');
				}
			});


			/*
			 *  Thumbnail helper. Disable animations, hide close button, arrows and slide to next gallery item if clicked
			 */

			$('.fancybox-thumbs').fancybox({
				prevEffect : 'none',
				nextEffect : 'none',

				closeBtn  : false,
				arrows    : false,
				nextClick : true,

				helpers : {
					thumbs : {
						width  : 50,
						height : 50
					}
				}
			});

			/*
			 *  Media helper. Group items, disable animations, hide arrows, enable media and button helpers.
			*/
			$('.fancybox-media')
				.attr('rel', 'media-gallery')
				.fancybox({
					openEffect : 'none',
					closeEffect : 'none',
					prevEffect : 'none',
					nextEffect : 'none',

					arrows : false,
					helpers : {
						media : {},
						buttons : {}
					}
				});

			/*
			 *  Open manually
			 */

			$("#fancybox-manual-a").click(function() {
				$.fancybox.open('1_b.jpg');
			});

			$("#fancybox-manual-b").click(function() {
				$.fancybox.open({
					href : 'iframe.html',
					type : 'iframe',
					padding : 5
				});
			});

			$("#fancybox-manual-c").click(function() {
				$.fancybox.open([
					{
						href : '1_b.jpg',
						title : 'My title'
					}, {
						href : '2_b.jpg',
						title : '2nd title'
					}, {
						href : '3_b.jpg'
					}
				], {
					helpers : {
						thumbs : {
							width: 75,
							height: 50
						}
					}
				});
			});


		});
	</script>

window.onscroll = function() {myFunction()};

var mobheader = document.getElementById("fixedhead");
var sticky = mobheader.offsetTop;

function myFunction() {
  if (document.body.scrollTop > 1 || document.documentElement.scrollTop > 1) {
    mobheader.classList.add("sticky");
  } else {
    mobheader.classList.remove("sticky");
  }
  
  
  
}

                          "" === n(this).attr("href") ||
                          "javascript:void(0)" === n(this).attr("href")
                        )
                          return !1
                        i.location.href = n(this).attr("href")
                      }
                    }))
      }
    ;(r.callback = function(n) {
      s[n] !== a && s[n].call(t)
    }),
      r.init()
  }),
    (n.fn.navigation = function(i) {
      return this.each(function() {
        if (a === n(this).data("navigation")) {
          var e = new n.navigation(this, i)
          n(this).data("navigation", e)
        }
      })
    })
})(jQuery, window, document)

;(function($) {
  "use strict"

  var $window = $(window)

  if ($.fn.navigation) {
    $("#navigation1").navigation()
    $("#always-hidden-nav").navigation({
      hidden: true
    })
  }

    $("#preloader").fadeOut("slow", function() {
      $(this).remove()
    })
  })

<script src="/assets/js/jquery.matchHeight.js"></script>
<script type="text/javascript">
$( document ).ready(function() {

	// Filter group toggle
	$('.cglv__sidebar__filters__group button').on('click', function(){
		$(this).parent().toggleClass('extended');
	})

	$('#mobile-filters-toggle').on('click', function(){
		$('.cglv__sidebar__filters').toggleClass('extended');
	})

	// Video popup on product-tile
	$('.video-popup').magnificPopup({
		type: 'iframe',
		mainClass: 'mfp-fade',
		removalDelay: 160,
		preloader: false,
		fixedContentPos: false
	});

	// Mobile filters toggle
	if ($(window).width() < 841) {

		var sidebarFilters = document.querySelector('.cglv__sidebar__filters');

		document.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
	  		moveNav(sidebarFilters);
	  		//console.log('scroll')
	  	});

	}

	// SEO content toggle
	$('#cglv-readmore-btn').on('click', function(){
		$('.cglv__intro__readmore-container').toggleClass('collapsed');

		if ($(this).attr('aria-expanded') == 'false') {
			$(this).attr('aria-expanded', 'true');
			$(this).text('Réduire');
		} else {
			$(this).attr('aria-expanded', 'false');
			$(this).text('Lire plus');
		}
	})
});

$( window ).resize(function() {

	if ($(window).width() > 840) {

		$('.cglv__sidebar__filters').removeClass('scrollup');
		$('.cglv__sidebar__filters').removeClass('extended');

	} else {

		document.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
	  		moveNav(document.querySelector('.cglv__sidebar__filters'));
	  	});
	}
});

var lastScrollTop =  pageYOffset || scrollTop;


// Fires when user scrolls on small devices
function moveNav(nav) {
	var filtersOffset = document.querySelector('.cglv__sidebar').getBoundingClientRect();
	var top = filtersOffset.top;

	var st = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop; // Credits: "https://github.com/qeremy/so/blob/master/so.dom.js#L426"


		nav.classList.remove("hide");
		nav.classList.remove("top");

		if (!nav.classList.contains("extended"))
			// nav.classList.remove("scrollup");

		if (($(window).width() < 841) && (top < 51)){
  		nav.classList.add("scrollup")
  		console.log('scrollup')
	} else {
		nav.classList.remove("scrollup")
	}

	if ($('.cglv__sidebar__filters').hasClass('scrollup')) {
		$('.cglv__sidebar').css('padding-top', '42px');
	} else {
		$('.cglv__sidebar').css('padding-top', '0');
	}

  	lastScrollTop = st <= 0 ? 0 : st; // For Mobile or negative scrolling
}
</script>

.view_mobile #bkt_qty {
	margin-left: 6px;
}
}
